                  <foreign lang="ar">بُؤْسَى</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">بَأْسَآءُ</foreign>: (TA, art. <foreign lang="ar">بأس</foreign>:) <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n44052-11" target="نَعْمَآءُ" n="11" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar" select="n44055"/>بَعْدَ ضَرَّآءَ</foreign>, in the Kur [xi. 13,] is like health after sickness; and richness, or competence, after want.                   <hi rend="ital">A blessing;</hi> (S;) <hi rend="ital">a cause of happiness.</hi> (K.) <hi rend="ital">A favour: a benefit; and the like.</hi> (S.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">نِعْمَةٌ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Wealth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">property.</hi> (K.) The first explanations given to it above are assigned in the K, not to this word, but to   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n44052-12" target="نَعِيمٌ" n="12" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n44056"/></foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n44052-13" target="نُعْمَى" n="13" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n44054"/></foreign>.          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">نِعْمَةٌ</foreign> with the article seems generally to signify <hi rend="ital">Wealth:</hi> and without the article, <hi rend="ital">A benefit, benefaction, favour, boon,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">blessing.</hi>
